/way 38.97, 70.53
/way 39, 59 right in from of the Warden's Vigil entrance you will see a big rock right next to 3x trees, stand on top of it and face the entrance of the Warden's Vigil. As long as you stand on the dark area in the middle of the rock and not too close to the edge of the rock, the secret fish should spawn 99% of the time somewhere on the road in front of the Warden's Vigil entrance. If you see the secret fish spawn behind you near the swamp area it's because you are standing to close to the edge of the rock.

/way 58.83 62.43) for better luck but mobs in the location doesn't seem to hyperspawn anymore. I had to wait for about 5 minutes after clearing the area for any of the mobs to respawn.
/way 58.83 62.43) worked great for farming these. On my guardian druid, I bought 10 of azure scrying crystals from the vendor that give the buff to increase the chance of the scrolls dropping there. In the small courtyard area near the waypoint, I ran around and pulled all of the mobs nearby outdoors, and they'd respawn in about the time it took me to aoe them down. After several minutes, I'd loot them, and if I got any scrolls, I'd use them and then use a scrying crystal to gain the buff and repeat. In 30-40 minutes of farming, I got 11 scrolls (one time two of them dropped in the time between my lootings), which got me 6 mysterious writings, 3 wondrous fish, and 2 draconic artifacts (I guess these mobs don't care much for the centaur tokens), as well as the item drops that can be crafted to summon the leatherworking, tailoring, engineering, and alchemy rares, as well as two of the items for the cooking rare. As a bonus, my druid is also my enchanter, so I was able to disenchant a dozen or so of the weapon, trinket, jewelry, and leather armor items from the 385 ilvl tokens to get a few resonant crystals.
/way 58.83, 62.43
/way 58.85,28.41 in Nazjatar for folks with coords. If no coords, look for Azsh'Ari Terrace on your map and head to a spot about 2 cms above the ARI in the name on the map (near the base of the  \"penis \" part of a watery area that looks a bit suggestive on the map, heh). The event takes place under the rocky roof, so fly in under it, where the naga mobs are. Look for 3 round pools of water close together. You will also see a pink skull icon on your map when it's active. If you're in the right spot, you'll hear an NPC boasting/harassing you and of course see the world quest pop up in your right-hand list.
